                <input type="hidden" name="pet" value=""/>

<script type="text/javascript">
    var newsletterSubscriberFormDetail = new VarienForm('newsletter-validate-detail');

    // prevent default submitting
    new Event.observe('newsletter-validate-detail', 'submit', function (e) {
        e.stop();
    });

    // function to use for reset form
    function resetInputForm(id) {
        jQuery(':input', '#' + id)
                .not(':button, :submit, #privacy')
                .val('')
                .removeAttr('checked')
                .removeAttr('selected');
    }

    // listen to onFormValidate and submit form only if validation succeeds
    newsletterSubscriberFormDetail.validator.options.onFormValidate = function (result, form) {

        if (result) {
            //handle animals
            var animals = [];
            jQuery('input:checked', '.check-animals').each(function () {
                animals.push(this.getValue());
            });
            var arrToString = animals.join(",");
            jQuery('input[name="pet"]').val(arrToString);

            // submit via ajax and ger errors if no success
            dataToSend = $('newsletter-validate-detail').serialize(true);
            dataToSend.mailchimp_dob = dataToSend.dob_day + "/" + dataToSend.dob_month + "/" + dataToSend.dob_year;
            dataToSend.mailchimp_animals = arrToString;

            new Ajax.Request("//www.ferplast.com/int/newsletter/subscriber/new/", {
                parameters: dataToSend,
                method: "post",
                onLoading: function () {
                    $('mc-embedded-subscribe').disabled = true;
                    $('mc-embedded-subscribe').addClassName('disactived');
                    $('newsletter-ajax-loading').removeClassName('hidden');
                },
                onComplete: function (transport) {
                    
                    $('mc-embedded-subscribe').disabled = false;
                    $('mc-embedded-subscribe').removeClassName('disactived');
                    $('newsletter-ajax-loading').addClassName('hidden');
                    $('mr_nl_messagesBlock').update(transport.responseJSON.messages);

                    if (transport.responseJSON.success !== false) {
                        resetInputForm("newsletter-validate-detail");
                        newsletterSubscriberFormDetail.validator.reset();
                    }
                },
                onSuccess: function (response) {
                    var animals = response.request.parameters.mailchimp_animals;
                    var newStr = "null";
                    if (animals) {
                        var re = /,/gi;
                        newStr = animals.replace(re,'|');
                    }
                    if (typeof dataLayer !== "undefined") {
                        dataLayer.push({
                            'event': 'newssubs',
                            'eventCategory': 'Newsletter_Suscription_' + response.request.parameters.country,
                            'eventAction': 'subscription_OK',
                            'eventLabel': 'Footer',
                            'type': newStr
                        });
                    }
                },
                onFailure: function () {
                    alert('Something went wrong...');
                }
            });
        }
    };
</script>    </div>

<script>

    jQuery(document).ready(function(){
        if (jQuery(window).width() < 768) {
            slideStoria();
            slideFooterIco();
        } else {
            jQuery('.bannerMilleTextRight.owl-carousel').owlCarousel('destroy');
            jQuery('.footerInformationContainer.owl-carousel').owlCarousel('destroy');
        }
        instagramWallSlider();
        youtubeWallSlider();
        enableWallSlider();
        videoStoriaBoxWidth();
    });

    jQuery(window).resize(function() {
        if (jQuery(window).width() < 768) {
            slideStoria();
            slideFooterIco();
        } else {
            jQuery('.bannerMilleTextRight.owl-carousel').owlCarousel('destroy');
            jQuery('.footerInformationContainer.owl-carousel').owlCarousel('destroy');
        }
        videoStoriaBoxWidth();
    });


    function slideStoria() {

        jQuery('.bannerMilleTextRight.owl-carousel').owlCarousel({
            loop:false,
            margin:0,
            responsiveClass:true,
            pagination:false,
            navigation:true,
            dots: true,
            responsive:{
                0:{
                    items:1,
                    pagination:false,
                    navigation:true,
                    dots: true
                },
                678:{
                    items:3,
                    nav:false
                }
            }
        });

    }

    function slideFooterIco() {

        jQuery('.footerInformationContainer.owl-carousel').owlCarousel({
            loop:false,
            margin:0,
            responsiveClass:true,
            pagination:false,
            navigation:true,
            dots: true,
            responsive:{
                0:{
                    items:1,
                    pagination:false,
                    navigation:true,
                    dots: true
                },
                678:{
                    items:3,
                    nav:false
                }
            }
        });

    }

    function instagramWallSlider() {

        jQuery('.instagramWall.owl-carousel').owlCarousel({

                }
            }
        });

    }

    function youtubeWallSlider() {

        jQuery('.youtubeWall.owl-carousel').owlCarousel({
            loop:true,
            margin:0,
            responsiveClass:true,
            pagination:false,
            navigation:true,
            dots: true,
            responsive:{

                    items:2,

    }


    function enableWallSlider() {

        jQuery(".instagramWallSlider").click(function(){
            if (!jQuery(this).hasClass("active")) {

                jQuery(this).addClass("active");
                jQuery(".youtubeWallSlider").removeClass("active");

                jQuery(".youtubeWallcontainer").hide();
                jQuery(".instagramWallcontainer").show();

                instagramWallSlider();

            }
        });

        jQuery(".youtubeWallSlider").click(function(){
            if (!jQuery(this).hasClass("active")) {

                jQuery(this).addClass("active");
                jQuery(".instagramWallSlider").removeClass("active");

                jQuery(".instagramWallcontainer").hide();
                jQuery(".youtubeWallcontainer").show();

                youtubeWallSlider();

            }
        });


    }

    function videoStoriaBoxWidth() {

        ytWidth = jQuery(".page-ferplast-company .main-container .main .col-main .company-top-container .company-image-top").width();
        jQuery(".videoStoriaBox").css("width",ytWidth);
        ytHeight = (ytWidth * 325) / 578;
        jQuery(".videoStoriaBox").css("height",ytHeight);

    }

    <script type="text/javascript">
        var freeProductsCheckFlag = false;
        var selectAllfreeProducts = function(txt){
            if (freeProductsCheckFlag == false) {
                $$('.free-product-checkbox').each(function(elem){
                    elem.checked = true;
                });
                freeProductsCheckFlag = true;
                txt.innerHTML= "unselect all";
            } else {
                $$('.free-product-checkbox').each(function(elem){
                    elem.checked = false;
                });
                freeProductsCheckFlag = false;
                txt.innerHTML= "select all";
            }
        }

        var initForm = function() {
            var freeProductToCartForm = new VarienForm('free-product-form');
            freeProductToCartForm.submit = function(){
                if (this.validator.validate()) {
                    this.form.submit();
                }
            }.bind(freeProductToCartForm);
            return freeProductToCartForm;
        }
    </script>


<script type="text/javascript">
    var validationForInvisibleCaptchaForm;
    var formToProtectOnPage;
    var formsToProtect;

    var onSubmit = function (token) {
            if (validationForInvisibleCaptchaForm.validator.validate()) {
                document.getElementById('amasty_invisible_token').setAttribute('value', token);
                document.getElementById('amasty_invisible_token').form.submit();
            } else {
                grecaptcha.reset();
            }
    };

    var onloadCallback = function () {
        var validationForInvisibleCaptchaForms = [];

        formsToProtect.forEach(function(currentFormId) {
            var currentForm = document.getElementById(currentFormId.replace("#",""));
            if (currentForm) {
                currentForm.innerHTML += '<input type="hidden" id="amasty_invisible_token" name="amasty_invisible_token" value=""/><input type="hidden" id="amasty_form_identifier" name="amasty_form_identifier" value="' + currentFormId.replace("#","") + '"/>'; 
                var buttonObj = currentForm.querySelector("[type='submit']");
		jQuery('#' + buttonObj.id).after('<div class="recaptcha_condition_form"><div class="recaptcha_message_box">Protetto da Invisible Recaptcha<br><a class="recaptcha_link" href="https://www.google.com/intl/it/policies/privacy/" target="_new_privacy">Privacy</a> | <a class="recaptcha_link" target="_new_terms" href="https://www.google.com/intl/it/policies/terms/">Condizioni</a></div></div>');
                validationForInvisibleCaptchaForms.push(new VarienForm(currentFormId.replace("#",""), false));
                
                jQuery('#amasty_invisible_token').parent().each(function(idx, el) {
                    var id = el.querySelector("[type='submit']");
                    grecaptcha.render(id, {
                        'sitekey': '6LcHwzwUAAAAALiO8M6KLnMZR0UOQHdpbC9UjdHd',
                        'callback': function(token) {
                            var form = new VarienForm(el.id, false);
                            if (form && form.validator.validate()) {
                                var elementForm = jQuery("#" + el.id + " :input[id='amasty_invisible_token']");
                                elementForm.val(token);
                                el.submit();
                            } else {
                                grecaptcha.reset();
                            }
                        },
                        'badge': 'inline'
                        });
                
                });
            }
        });
    };

    formsToProtect = ["#contactForm","#review-form","#form-validate"];
    formsToProtect.forEach(function(item) {
        formToProtect = $$(item)[0];
	
        if (formToProtect) {
            formToProtectOnPage = formToProtect;
        }
    });

    if (formToProtectOnPage) {
        var recaptchaScript = document.createElement('script');
        recaptchaScript.src = 'https://www.google.com/recaptcha/api.js?onload=onloadCallback&render=explicit';
        recaptchaScript.attributes = 'async defer';
        document.body.appendChild(recaptchaScript);
        var errorPanel = document.getElementsByClassName("messages");
        if (errorPanel.length > 0) {
            var currentSelectedForm = "";
            formsToProtect.forEach(function(item) {
                if (currentSelectedForm == item.replace("#","")) {
                    var formToProtectOnPage = document.getElementById(item.replace("#",""));
                    formToProtectOnPage.parentNode.insertBefore(errorPanel[0], formToProtectOnPage);
                }
            });
        }
    }

</script>

    <div class="cookiepolicy-dropdown" style="background-color:#666666; color:#ffffff;  ">
        <div class="block-cookiepolicy">
            <div class="block-content">
                <p>
                    This website uses his "cookies" to improve your own browsing experience and third party cookies to send promotional messages in line with your preferences. For more information and modify your cookie settings, <a href="customer-care#cookies" target="_blank">click here</a>. If you click on the “OK” button or continue to browse on this site, you consent to use our cookies.                </p>
                <button class="accept">OK</button>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        var topCookiePolicy = function () {
            var cookiepolicyHide = jQuery.cookie("cookiepolicy_accepted");
            if (cookiepolicyHide !== "yes" || !cookiesEnabled()) { //policy not accepted OR cookies disabled
                jQuery('.cookiepolicy-dropdown').show();
            }
        };

        var cookiesEnabled = function () {
            var cookieEnabled = !!(navigator.cookieEnabled);

            if (typeof navigator.cookieEnabled == "undefined" && !cookieEnabled) {
                document.cookie = "testcookie";
                cookieEnabled = (document.cookie.indexOf("testcookie") != -1);
            }
            return (cookieEnabled);
        };

        jQuery(document).ready(function () {
            topCookiePolicy();

            var cookieAccept = jQuery('.cookiepolicy-dropdown button.accept, .cookiepolicy-dropdown .block-content a');
            var cookieBlock = jQuery('.cookiepolicy-dropdown');

                        cookieAccept.on('click', function () {
                cookieBlock.fadeOut('slow');
                jQuery.cookie('cookiepolicy_accepted', 'yes', {expires: 365, path: '/'});
            });
                    });
    </script>
            </div>
        </div>
            </body>
</html>
